We request SEBI to order a thorough investigation in this matter and immediately prevent / restrain Credit Suisse from selling the Prime Focus Shares as the sale of equity shares of Prime Focus Limited below the intrinsic value would be illegal, in breach of fiduciary duties, and will be substantially prejudicial to the stakeholders of the Company including its 8 lakh shareholders and lenders (including LIC of India, GIC, New India Assurance, EPFO, Army Group Insurance Fund, MSEB Provident Fund). '.
